 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="line-height:1.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">March&nbsp;23, 2022 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GENERAL MILLS REPORTS FISCAL 2022 THIRD-QUARTER RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>AND RAISES FULL-YEAR OUTLOOK </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales essentially matched <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results at $4.5&nbsp;billion;
organic net sales<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP> were up 4&nbsp;percent </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit declined 1&nbsp;percent to $815&nbsp;million; adjusted operating profit was down
6&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted earnings per share (EPS) of $1.08 increased 13&nbsp;percent from the prior year; adjusted diluted EPS
of $0.84 increased 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>&#149;</B></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Company raises full-year fiscal 2022 outlook </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I>&sup1;</I></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left"><I>Please see Note 8 to the Consolidated Financial Statements below for reconciliation of this and other <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures used in this release. </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">MINNEAPOLIS, Minn. &#150; March&nbsp;23,
2022 &#150; General Mills (NYSE: GIS) today reported results for the third quarter ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our solid
execution in a highly volatile environment enabled us to close the third quarter with improved momentum,&#148; said General Mills Chairman and Chief Executive Officer Jeff Harmening. &#147;Demand for our brands remains robust, and our team has shown
great agility to overcome disruptions throughout the supply chain and deliver for our customers and consumers. We expect to drive strong growth in the fourth quarter, fueled by accelerating net price realization. With confidence in our plans and
positive momentum on our business, we&#146;re raising our guidance for fiscal 2022.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills is executing its Accelerate
strategy to drive sustainable, profitable growth and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-tier</FONT> shareholder returns over the long term. The strategy focuses on four pillars to create competitive advantages and win: boldly building brands,
relentlessly innovating, unleashing scale, and being a force for good. The company is prioritizing its core markets, global platforms, and local gem brands that have the best prospects for profitable growth and is committed to reshaping its
portfolio with strategic acquisitions and divestitures, including its recent pet treats acquisition and European yogurt and dough divestitures, to further enhance its growth profile. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills expects changes in consumer behaviors driven by the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic will result in ongoing elevated consumer demand for food at home, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels. These changes include more time spent working from home
and increased consumer appreciation for cooking and baking. In addition, an increase in the pet population and further humanization and premiumization of pet food during the pandemic are expected to create tailwinds for the pet food category. The
company plans to capitalize on these opportunities, addressing evolving consumer needs through its leading brands, innovation, and advantaged capabilities to generate profitable growth. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Third Quarter Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> were essentially flat to last year at $4.5&nbsp;billion, including a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">3-point</FONT> net headwind from divestiture and acquisition activity. Organic net sales increased 4&nbsp;percent, reflecting 7 points of positive organic net price realization and mix, partially offset by a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">4-point</FONT> headwind from lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 350 basis points to 30.9&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs and
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross margin was down 160 basis points to 31.4&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by input cost inflation, supply chain deleverage, and higher other cost of goods sold, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and Holistic Margin Management (HMM) cost savings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $815&nbsp;million was down 1&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by lower gross profit
dollars and less favorable investment activity, partially offset by a gain on divestitures.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 18.0&nbsp;percent was down 30 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit declined 6&nbsp;percent, driven by
lower adjusted gross profit dollars. Adjusted operating profit margin decreased 90 basis points to 14.9&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were up 11&nbsp;percent to $660&nbsp;million and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was up 13&nbsp;percent to $1.08, driven primarily by a lower adjusted tax rate and lower net interest expense. Adjusted diluted EPS of $0.84 increased 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by lower net interest expense,
higher <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures, and lower net earnings attributable to redeemable and noncontrolling interests, partially offset by lower adjusted operating profit. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis</B>, relative to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, third-quarter results included: net sales up 4&nbsp;percent and organic net sales up 5&nbsp;percent; operating profit up 12&nbsp;percent and adjusted operating profit down 1&nbsp;percent in
constant currency; and diluted EPS up 21&nbsp;percent and constant-currency adjusted diluted EPS up 4&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Nine Month
Results Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net sales</B> increased 4&nbsp;percent to $14.1&nbsp;billion, including 1 point of favorable foreign currency
exchange and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> net headwind from divestiture and acquisition activity. Organic net sales increased 4&nbsp;percent, reflecting 5 points of positive organic net price realization and mix, partially
offset by a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-point</FONT> headwind from lower organic pound volume. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Gross margin</B> was down 300 basis points to 32.8&nbsp;percent of net sales, driven by higher input costs and
unfavorable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. Adjusted gross margin was down 210 basis points to 32.8&nbsp;percent of
net sales, driven by input cost inflation, supply chain deleverage, and higher other cost of goods sold, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and HMM cost savings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Operating profit </B>of $2.5&nbsp;billion was down 5&nbsp;percent, driven primarily by lower gross profit
dollars, partially offset by lower selling, general, and administrative (SG&amp;A) expenses.<B> Operating profit margin</B> of 17.4&nbsp;percent was down 170 basis points. Constant-currency adjusted operating profit declined 5&nbsp;percent, driven
by lower adjusted gross profit dollars, partially offset by lower adjusted SG&amp;A expenses. Adjusted operating profit margin decreased 130 basis points to 16.4&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net earnings attributable to General Mills</B> were down 2&nbsp;percent to $1.9&nbsp;billion and <B>diluted
EPS</B> was down 1&nbsp;percent to $3.07, primarily reflecting lower operating profit, partially offset by lower net interest expense and a effective tax rate. Adjusted diluted EPS of $2.82 was down 2&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven
primarily by lower adjusted operating profit, partially offset by lower net interest expense. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis</B>, relative to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, nine-month results included: net sales and organic net sales each up 6&nbsp;percent; operating profit up 8&nbsp;percent and adjusted operating profit up 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency;
diluted EPS up 10&nbsp;percent and adjusted diluted EPS up 6&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Operating Segment Results
</U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, General Mills announced a new organization structure to streamline its global operations. As a result of
these changes, beginning in the third quarter of fiscal 2022, the company is reporting results for its four operating segments as follows: North America Retail, Pet, North America Foodservice, and International. Net sales by segment and segment
operating profit amounts have been restated to reflect the new operating segments <I>(please see Note 2 below for more information on our operating segments)</I>. </P>

<TD>&nbsp;</TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Retail Segment </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for General Mills&#146; North America Retail segment increased 1&nbsp;percent to $2.81&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix, partially offset by lower pound volume. Organic net sales were 1&nbsp;percent above <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that grew 11&nbsp;percent. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound
growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, third-quarter organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent. Net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent in U.S. Morning Foods, which represents the combination of the previous
U.S. Cereal and U.S. Yogurt units, and up 3&nbsp;percent in U.S. Snacks. Net sales for the U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions and Canada units were each down 2&nbsp;percent. Net sales performance lagged Nielsen-measured retail sales growth by
approximately 3 points in the quarter, driven by supply shortages on the refrigerated dough, pizza, and hot snacks categories. The company took actions to address the shortages and drove notable improvement in customer service levels on those
platforms in the final weeks of the quarter. Segment operating profit of $612&nbsp;million was down 3&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net price
realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was up 5&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America Retail segment net sales were essentially in line with
last year at $8.57&nbsp;billion. Organic net sales were flat to last year. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month organic net sales were up 6&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $1.94&nbsp;billion
was down 7&nbsp;percent as reported and in constant currency, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. On a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month segment operating profit was up 3&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Pet Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the Pet segment
increased 30&nbsp;percent to $568&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and strong volume growth. Net sales results in the quarter included a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">14-point</FONT> benefit from the pet treats
acquisition. Organic net sales were up 16&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 8&nbsp;percent to $111&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, including benefits from the pet treats
acquisition, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, Pet segment net sales increased
28&nbsp;percent to $1.65&nbsp;billion, driven by favorable net price realization and mix and positive contributions from volume growth. Organic net sales were up 16&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 15&nbsp;percent to
$357&nbsp;million, driven primarily by favorable net price realization and mix and higher volume, including benefits from the pet treats acquisition, partially offset by higher input costs and higher SG&amp;A expenses. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>North America Foodservice Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net
sales for the North America Foodservice segment increased 22&nbsp;percent to $437&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price realization and mix, including market index pricing on bakery flour, and positive contributions from volume growth. On a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, relative to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels, third-quarter net sales were down 3&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit decreased 13&nbsp;percent to
$35&nbsp;million, driven by higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment operating profit was down 29&nbsp;percent. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">5 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, North America Foodservice net sales increased 24&nbsp;percent to
$1.32&nbsp;billion. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month net sales were down 4&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit increased 27&nbsp;percent to $175&nbsp;million, driven by favorable net price
realization and mix and higher volume, partially offset by higher input costs. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month segment operating profit was down 13&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>International Segment </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for the
International segment were down 23&nbsp;percent to $721&nbsp;million, including a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">20-point</FONT> headwind from the divestitures of the European yogurt and dough businesses and 2 points of unfavorable foreign
currency exchange. Organic net sales were down 1&nbsp;percent, reflecting a difficult comparison to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> results that were up 10&nbsp;percent. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound
growth basis, third-quarter organic net sales were up 4&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $36&nbsp;million was down 13&nbsp;percent as reported and down 16&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven primarily by lower volume, including the
impact of the European yogurt and dough divestitures, and higher input costs, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, segment
operating profit was up 1&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Through nine months, International net sales declined 5&nbsp;percent to
$2.57&nbsp;billion, including an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-point</FONT> headwind from the divestitures of the European yogurt and dough businesses and 1 point of favorable foreign currency exchange. Organic net sales were up 1&nbsp;percent.
On a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month organic net sales were up 5&nbsp;percent. Segment operating profit of $156&nbsp;million was down 14&nbsp;percent as reported and down 18&nbsp;percent in constant
currency, driven primarily by higher input costs and lower volume, including the impact of the European yogurt and dough divestitures, partially offset by favorable net price realization and mix and lower SG&amp;A expenses. On a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, nine-month segment operating profit was up 5&nbsp;percent in constant currency. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Joint Venture Summary </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Third-quarter net sales for
Cereal Partners Worldwide (CPW) were up 1&nbsp;percent in constant currency, driven by positive net price realization and mix, partially offset by lower volume. Constant-currency net sales increased 9&nbsp;percent for
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">H&auml;agen-Dazs</FONT> Japan (HDJ), driven by strong core performance and improved distribution. Combined <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures were $30&nbsp;million compared
to $12&nbsp;million a year ago, driven by higher profit at CPW. Through nine months, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures increased 3&nbsp;percent to $92&nbsp;million. On a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> compound growth basis, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings from joint ventures were up 66&nbsp;percent in the third quarter and up 27&nbsp;percent through nine months. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">6 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Other Income Statement Items </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate items totaled $141&nbsp;million net expense in the third quarter of fiscal 2022, compared to $24&nbsp;million of income a year ago.
Excluding <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation effects and other items affecting comparability, unallocated corporate items totaled $117&nbsp;million net expense this year compared
to $98&nbsp;million net expense last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company recorded a net $170&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT>
gain on divestitures in the third quarter <I>(please see Note 3 below for more information on these items)</I>. Restructuring, impairment, and other exit costs totaled $7&nbsp;million in the third quarter compared to $11&nbsp;million a year ago. An
additional $2&nbsp;million of restructuring and project-related charges was recorded in cost of sales this year compared to $1&nbsp;million a year ago <I>(please see Note 4 below for more information on these charges)</I>. <I></I> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net interest expense totaled $86&nbsp;million in the third quarter compared to $106&nbsp;million a year ago, driven primarily by lower average
long-term debt balances. The effective tax rate in the quarter was 16.3&nbsp;percent compared to 21.5&nbsp;percent last year <I>(please see Note 7 below for more information on our effective tax rate)</I>. The adjusted effective tax rate was
21.0&nbsp;percent compared to 21.6&nbsp;percent a year ago. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Cash Flow Generation and Cash Returns </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Cash provided by operating activities increased 1&nbsp;percent to $2.23&nbsp;billion through nine months of fiscal 2022, driven primarily by changes in
inventories, partially offset by a gain on divestitures, changes in accounts payable, and lower net earnings. Capital investments of $351&nbsp;million were up 1&nbsp;percent from a year ago. Dividends paid essentially matched <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> levels at $934&nbsp;million. General Mills repurchased approximately 8.8&nbsp;million shares of common stock through nine months of fiscal 2022 for a total of $550&nbsp;million. Average diluted shares
outstanding decreased 1&nbsp;percent to 614&nbsp;million. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">7 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Fiscal 2022 Outlook </U></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General Mills raised its guidance for fiscal 2022 to reflect <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-date</FONT></FONT>
performance and an outlook for strong <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">top-</FONT> and bottom-line growth in the fourth quarter. The company&#146;s updated full-year fiscal 2022 financial targets are summarized below: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Organic net sales</B> are now expected to increase approximately 5&nbsp;percent, including an expectation for
organic net price realization and mix to increase sequentially from the third quarter to the fourth quarter. Full-year organic net sales were previously expected to increase 4 to 5&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

reflecting the increased guidance on organic net sales. For the full year, the company continues to expect input cost inflation of 8 to 9&nbsp;percent and significant costs related to supply chain disruptions. Adjusted operating profit was
previously expected to decline 4 to 1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

driven by the higher outlook on adjusted operating profit. Adjusted diluted EPS were previously expected to range between down 2&nbsp;percent and up 1&nbsp;percent. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">after-tax</FONT> earnings. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

Central time (7:30 a.m. Eastern time) and will hold a live, webcasted question and answer session beginning at 8:00 a.m. Central time (9:00 a.m. Eastern time). The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-recorded</FONT> remarks and the webcast will be

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">GENERAL MILLS, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">NOTES TO CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL STATEMENTS </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(Unaudited) </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(1)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The accompanying Consolidated Financial Statements of General Mills, Inc. (we, us, our, General Mills, or the
Company) have been prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States for annual and interim financial information. In the opinion of management, all adjustments considered necessary for a fair presentation
have been included and are of a normal recurring nature. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(2)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed a new organization structure to streamline our global
operations. This global reorganization required us to reevaluate our operating segments. Under our new organization structure, our chief operating decision maker assesses performance and makes decisions about resources to be allocated to our
operating segments as follows: North America Retail; International; Pet; and North America Foodservice. We have restated our net sales by segment and segment operating profit amounts to reflect our new operating segments. These segment changes had
no effect on previously reported consolidated net sales, operating profit, net earnings attributable to General Mills, or earnings per share. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our North America Retail operating segment includes convenience store businesses from our former Convenience Stores&nbsp;&amp; Foodservice
segment. Within our North America Retail operating segment, our former U.S. Cereal operating unit and U.S. Yogurt operating unit have been combined into the U.S. Morning Foods operating unit. Additionally, the U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking Solutions
operating unit combines the former U.S. Meals&nbsp;&amp; Baking operating unit with certain businesses from the U.S. Snacks operating unit. The Canada operating unit excludes Canada foodservice businesses which are now included in our North America
Foodservice operating segment. The resulting North America Foodservice operating segment exclusively includes our foodservice businesses. Our International operating segment combines our former Europe&nbsp;&amp; Australia and Asia&nbsp;&amp; Latin
America operating segments. Our Pet operating segment is unchanged. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(3)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">During the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we completed the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques
SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal International (Sodiaal) in exchange for Sodiaal&#146;s interest in our Canadian yogurt business, a modified agreement for the use of Yoplait and Libert&eacute; brands in the United States and
Canada, and cash. We recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain of $149&nbsp;million on the sale of these businesses during the third quarter of fiscal 2022. These transactions are subject to sale price adjustments in future
periods that could impact the net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of
fiscal 2022, we entered into definitive agreements to sell our European dough businesses. During the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we recorded a net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-tax</FONT> gain on sale of $21&nbsp;million related to certain
of these agreements and the remaining transactions are expected to close by the end of fiscal 2022, subject to appropriate labor consultations, regulatory approvals, and other customary closing conditions. The associated assets and liabilities have
an immaterial impact on the presentation of our Consolidated Balance Sheets as of February&nbsp;27, 2022. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first quarter of
fiscal 2022, we acquired the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business for $1.2&nbsp;billion in cash. We financed the transaction with a combination of cash on hand and short-term debt. We consolidated the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business into our
Consolidated Balance Sheets and recorded goodwill of $759&nbsp;million, indefinite-lived intangible assets for the <I>Nudges</I>, <I>Top Chews</I> and <I>True Chews</I> brands totaling $330&nbsp;million in aggregate, and a finite-lived customer
relationship asset of $40&nbsp;million. The goodwill is included in the Pet reporting unit and is deductible for tax purposes. The pro forma effects of this acquisition were not material. We have conducted a preliminary assessment of the fair value
of the acquired assets and liabilities of the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business. The consolidated results of the Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business are reported in our Pet operating segment on a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-month</FONT> lag. Accordingly, our Consolidated Statements of Earnings include seven months of operating results for the acquired business for the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. In the third
quarter of fiscal 2022, we recorded a purchase price adjustment that resulted in a $3&nbsp;million increase to goodwill. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(5)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Unallocated corporate expense totaled $141&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to
$24&nbsp;million of income in the same period in fiscal 2021. We recorded a $20&nbsp;million net increase in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain
commodity positions and grain inventories in the third quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to a $56&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the same period last year. We recorded $11&nbsp;million of net gains related to the sale of certain corporate
investments and valuation adjustments in the third quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to $59&nbsp;million in the third quarter of fiscal 2021. In the third quarter of fiscal 2022, we recorded $4&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our
acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and $9&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and a European dough business. We recorded
$2&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in cost of sales in the third quarter of fiscal 2022 compared to $1&nbsp;million in the same period last year. We also recorded an $8&nbsp;million favorable adjustment related to a product recall in our
international Green Giant business in the third quarter of fiscal 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unallocated corporate expense totaled
$329&nbsp;million in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, compared to $98&nbsp;million in the same period last year. We recorded a $16&nbsp;million net decrease in expense related to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> valuation of certain commodity positions and grain inventories in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, compared to a $118&nbsp;million net decrease in expense in the same period
last year. We recorded $21&nbsp;million of net gains related to the sale of corporate investments and valuation adjustments in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, compared to $78&nbsp;million in the same period last year. In the
nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, we recorded $20&nbsp;million of integration costs related to our acquisition of Tyson Foods&#146; pet treats business and $57&nbsp;million of transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in
Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl and a European dough business. In addition, we recorded a $20&nbsp;million recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item and a $13&nbsp;million insurance recovery in the
nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022. We also recorded $3&nbsp;million of restructuring charges in costs of sales, compared to $2&nbsp;million in the same period last year. </P>

<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Incremental shares from stock options, restricted stock units, and performance share units are computed by the
treasury stock method. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(7)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The effective tax rate for the third quarter of fiscal 2022 was 16.3&nbsp;percent compared to 21.5&nbsp;percent
for the same period last year. The 5.2 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-taxable</FONT> components of divestiture gains and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction, partially offset
by certain discrete tax benefits recorded in the third quarter of fiscal 2021. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 21.0&nbsp;percent in the quarter ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, compared to 21.6&nbsp;percent in
the same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; section below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.6 percentage point decrease was primarily due to favorable
changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction, partially offset by certain discrete tax benefits recorded in the third quarter of fiscal 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The effective tax rate for the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, was 19.9&nbsp;percent compared to 22.0&nbsp;percent for the same
period last year. The 2.1 percentage point decrease was primarily due to certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-taxable</FONT> components of the divestitures gains and favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2022, partially
offset by certain discrete benefits in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;28, 2021. Our effective tax rate excluding certain items affecting comparability was 21.7&nbsp;percent in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;27, 2022, compared
to 21.9&nbsp;percent in the same period last year (see the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">&#147;Non-GAAP</FONT> Measures&#148; section below for a description of our use of measures not defined by GAAP). The 0.2 percentage point decrease is
primarily due to favorable changes in earnings mix by jurisdiction in fiscal 2022, partially offset by certain discrete benefits in the nine-month period ended February&nbsp;28, 2021. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(8)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">We have included measures in this release that are not defined by GAAP. We believe that these measures provide
useful information to investors and include these measures in other communications to investors. For each of these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, we are providing below a reconciliation of the differences
between the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure and the most directly comparable GAAP measure, an explanation of why we believe the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure provides useful information to
investors and any additional material purposes for which our management or Board of Directors uses the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure. These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures should be viewed in
addition to, and not in lieu of, the comparable GAAP measure. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">15 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We provide organic net sales growth rates for our consolidated net sales and segment net
sales. This measure is used in reporting to our Board of Directors and executive management and as a component of the Board of Directors&#146; measurement of our performance for incentive compensation purposes. We believe that organic net sales
growth rates provide useful information to investors because they provide transparency to underlying performance in our net sales by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a
53rd&nbsp;fiscal week, when applicable, have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> comparability. A reconciliation of these measures to reported net sales growth rates, the relevant GAAP
measures, are included in our Operating Segment Results above. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain measures in this release are presented excluding the impact of
foreign currency exchange (constant-currency). To present this information, current period results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are translated into United States dollars at the average exchange rates in
effect during the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year, rather than the actual average exchange rates in effect during the current fiscal year. Therefore, the foreign currency impact is equal to current year results in local currencies
multiplied by the change in the average foreign currency exchange rate between the current fiscal period and the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year. We believe that these constant-currency measures provide useful information to investors
because they provide transparency to underlying performance by excluding the effect that foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations have on <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">period-to-period</FONT></FONT>
comparability given volatility in foreign currency exchange markets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Also, certain measures in this release are presented on an adjusted
basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in management&#146;s judgment, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT>
assessment of operating results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our fiscal 2022 outlook for organic net sales growth, adjusted operating profit growth, adjusted diluted
EPS growth, and free cash flow conversion are <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures that exclude, or have otherwise been adjusted for, items impacting comparability, including the effect of foreign currency exchange
rate fluctuations, acquisitions, divestitures, and a 53rd week, when applicable. We are not able to reconcile these forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures to their most directly comparable forward-looking
GAAP financial measure without unreasonable efforts because we are unable to predict with a reasonable degree of certainty the actual impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates or the timing of acquisitions and divestitures throughout
fiscal 2022. The unavailable information could have a significant impact on our fiscal 2022 GAAP financial results. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For fiscal 2022, we
currently expect: foreign currency exchange rates (based on a blend of forward and forecasted rates and hedge positions) and acquisitions and divestitures to decrease net sales by approximately 1 point; foreign currency exchange rates to have an
immaterial impact on adjusted operating profit and adjusted diluted EPS growth; and restructuring charges and project-related costs and transaction costs and acquisition integration costs to total approximately $110&nbsp;million to
$150&nbsp;million. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Significant Items Impacting Comparability </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Several measures below are presented on an adjusted basis. The adjustments are either items resulting from infrequently occurring events or items that, in
management&#146;s judgement, significantly affect the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> assessment of operating results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following are descriptions of significant items impacting comparability of our results. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Divestitures gain</U> </P>

and the sale of a European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Transaction costs</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Transaction costs related to the sale of our interests in Yoplait SAS, Yoplait Marques SNC, and Libert&eacute; Marques S&agrave;rl to Sodiaal
and the sale of our European dough businesses in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 3. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-income</FONT> tax
recovery</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recovery related to a Brazil indirect tax item recorded in fiscal 2022. Please see Note 5. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> effects</U> </P>

recognized in unallocated corporate items. Please see Note 5. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Restructuring charges</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Restructuring charges for International supply chain optimization actions and previously announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2022.
Restructuring charges for previously announced restructuring actions in fiscal 2021. Please see Note 4. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Product recall</U> </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Organic Net Sales on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT> Compound Growth Rate Basis </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors as it compares our organic net sales growth in fiscal 2022 to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels of activity in fiscal 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Organic net sales on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-year</FONT>
compound growth rate basis are calculated as follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="92%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

Growth Rate Basis</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe that this measure provides useful information to investors as it compares our constant-currency segment operating profit
growth in fiscal 2022 to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-pandemic</FONT> levels of activity in fiscal 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Our segments&#146; constant-currency

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><U>Adjusted Effective Income Tax Rate </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We believe this measure provides useful information to investors because it presents the adjusted effective income tax rate on a comparable <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-to-year</FONT></FONT> basis. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted effective income tax rates are calculated as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
